Pleiades Change Log: 2012-08-01 - 2012-08-31

New Place Resources

  • Bawtry Roman fort
    Site of mid- to late-fourth century Roman fort.
    Creators: Scott Vanderbilt
    Contributors: Jeffrey Becker
  • Kenan Tepe
    Ancient site on the Tigris river in Turkey
    Creators: Francis Deblauwe
    Contributors: Sean Gillies, Tom Elliott, Tom Elliott
  • Maison Carrée
    A well preserved Roman temple built ca. 16 B.C. and dedicated to Caius and Lucius Caesar.
    Creators: Sean Gillies, Tom Elliott
    Contributors: Jeffrey Becker
  • Shaduppum
    Shaduppum was a small but heavily fortified city dating from the middle of the third millennium to the second millennium B.C.
    Creators: Jeffrey Becker
    Contributors: Sean Gillies, Francis Deblauwe, B. Siewert-Mayer, Eric Kansa, W. Röllig, Tom Elliott, H. Kopp
  • Tour Magne
    Situated atop Mount Cavalier, the so-called "Tour Magne" is a tower on the fortified walls of ancient Nemausus. The tower dates to the time of Augustus.
    Creators: Sean Gillies, Tom Elliott
    Contributors: Jeffrey Becker

Modified Place Resources

  • Abia
    An ancient settlement, attested by literary or documentary sources, whose precise location cannot be determined today
    Creators: J. McK. Camp II, G. Reger
    Contributors: R. Talbert, Tom Elliott, Sean Gillies
    Modifications: whittling away at unlocated places. see http://pleiades.stoa.org/docs/content-development-projects/whittle-away-at-unlocated-places for more details.
    Actors: Sean Gillies
  • Acantion
    An ancient island or island group, attested by literary or documentary sources, whose precise location cannot be determined today
    Creators: E.N. Borza
    Contributors: G. Reger, R. Talbert, Tom Elliott, Sean Gillies
    Modifications: whittling away at unlocated places. see http://pleiades.stoa.org/docs/content-development-projects/whittle-away-at-unlocated-places for more details.
    Actors: Sean Gillies
  • Acerrae Vafriae
    An ancient settlement of Umbria that is attested in Pliny the Elder but is recorded as a place that had vanished by his own day.
    Creators: W.V. Harris
    Contributors: R. Talbert, Sean Gillies, Tom Elliott, Jeffrey Becker
    Modifications: whittling away at unlocated places. see http://pleiades.stoa.org/docs/content-development-projects/whittle-away-at-unlocated-places for more details.
    Actors: Sean Gillies
  • Aceste

    Actors: Sean Gillies
  • Achaia (settlement)
    An ancient settlement, said by Strabo to have been located in Areia (i.e., in or near the modern province of Herat, Afghanistan). Its precise location is unknown.
    Creators: M.U. Erdosy
    Contributors: R. Talbert, Sean Gillies, Tom Elliott, Jeffrey Becker
    Modifications: whittling away at unlocated places. see http://pleiades.stoa.org/docs/content-development-projects/whittle-away-at-unlocated-places for more details.
    Actors: Sean Gillies

  • Larisa
    An ancient settlement, described by Strabo as lying "on the left of the Pontus, between Naulochus and Odessos, near Mount Haimos". Its modern location is uncertain, although it may correspond to a fortified settlement on the St. Athanasius Cape near modern Byala in Bulgaria.

  • Temple of Athena Alea at Tegea
